                   {     \ `-.,-.,-' /     }   on some screens.  It depends
                  {'      \  (   )  /      `}  on the positioning of the ~.
                  {'       \.-`-'-./       `}  For some screens, the ~ is
                  `{      .'       `.      }'  about midway down the char.
                   `{     : :_,.._; :     }'   position.  That's how it is
                   {'     `:__(|)==:'     `}   on mine at the moment.
                  {'     /  /     \  \     `}
           (     /  /       \  \     )  Otherwise, the halo and the
                  `-..-'   |       |   `-..-'  tips of the wings may want a
                           |       |           little diddling.
